\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Clamp\ float\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a19c1202d4696b35627119b67a344dc44}{RMAPI}}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a0b07a45c6e21093f520658daecd01f36}{Clamp}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ min,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ max)}

\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Calculate\ linear\ interpolation\ between\ two\ floats}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a19c1202d4696b35627119b67a344dc44}{RMAPI}}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_aae383c100851880be4e0ebdc93e63126}{Lerp}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a60de64d75454385b23995437f1d72669}{start}},\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ end,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ amount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00179\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00180\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ result\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a60de64d75454385b23995437f1d72669}{start}}\ +\ amount*(end\ -\/\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a60de64d75454385b23995437f1d72669}{start}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{00181\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}

\DoxyCodeLine{00184\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00185\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Normalize\ input\ value\ within\ input\ range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00186\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a19c1202d4696b35627119b67a344dc44}{RMAPI}}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a5addef0c374207a9592172a53378a704}{Normalize}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a60de64d75454385b23995437f1d72669}{start}},\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ end)}

\DoxyCodeLine{00188\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ result\ =\ (value\ -\/\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a60de64d75454385b23995437f1d72669}{start}})/(end\ -\/\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a60de64d75454385b23995437f1d72669}{start}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Remap\ input\ value\ within\ input\ range\ to\ output\ range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00194\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a19c1202d4696b35627119b67a344dc44}{RMAPI}}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_aedcf4bebe646ff13ffda8a8b2c52ba4f}{Remap}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ inputStart,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ inputEnd,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ outputStart,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ outputEnd)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00195\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00196\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ result\ =\ (value\ -\/\ inputStart)/(inputEnd\ -\/\ inputStart)*(outputEnd\ -\/\ outputStart)\ +\ outputStart;}

\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Wrap\ input\ value\ from\ min\ to\ max}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a19c1202d4696b35627119b67a344dc44}{RMAPI}}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a860599a4d89fb83090024811f068f114}{Wrap}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ value,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ min,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ max)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ result\ =\ value\ -\/\ (max\ -\/\ min)*floorf((value\ -\/\ min)/(max\ -\/\ min));}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Check\ whether\ two\ given\ floats\ are\ almost\ equal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a19c1202d4696b35627119b67a344dc44}{RMAPI}}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a41ac641607e78233960eaf5cc545777a}{FloatEquals}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ x,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}\ y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ result\ =\ (fabsf(x\ -\/\ y))\ <=\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{raymath_8h_a002b2f4894492820fe708b1b7e7c5e70}{EPSILON}}*fmaxf(1.0f,\ fmaxf(fabsf(x),\ fabsf(y))));}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \}}
